Cartographer: 
- Also do WorldMapFrame:SetAttribute("UIPanelLayout-enabled, false) when removing the WorldMapFrame from UIPanel's control. As of late, this is the attribute that the UIPanel code looks at to determine if a frame is under its control.
Normally, this does not cause problems, but if the map is shown prior to Carto loading, these attributes get set. QuestHistory does a quick show+hide on startup, and hey presto, bug.

r1531 | ckknight | 2007-06-17 03:23:46 +0000 (Sun, 17 Jun 2007) | 1 line

Cartographer - optimize the guild spammer slightly
------------------------------------------------------------------------
r1530 | ckknight | 2007-06-17 02:41:20 +0000 (Sun, 17 Jun 2007) | 3 lines
Changed paths:
   M /tmp/trunk/Cartographer/Cartographer.lua
   M /tmp/trunk/Cartographer/Cartographer_GuildPositions/GuildPositions.lua

Cartographer - change the guildSpammer from a push situation to a pull, e.g. when someone opens their map, they request position for that zone/continent. They also request again every 5 seconds (or more depending on guild members) or whenever they change zones/continents. On the other end, when a request is received, a whisper is sent to the other person detailing the position.
Note: This will receive old guild spams from previous versions, but previous versions will not be able to see the new positions.
This causes _significantly_ less addon traffic overall.
------------------------------------------------------------------------

r1442 | ckknight | 2007-05-11 06:12:19 +0000 (Fri, 11 May 2007) | 3 lines

Cartographer_InstanceMaps - upgraded for WoW 2.1
- currently Data.lua has both the WoW 2.0 and WoW 2.1 versions.
- basically, apparently Blizzard now loads textures lazily instead of directly on-the-fly. This means that their height/width is not available until a few frames later. Since Cartographer_InstanceMaps depends on this information, it now does some mad hax to delay itself until the textures are fully loaded.

Cartographer-Notes - added corner support.
if GetMinimapShape() returns "CORNER-TOPRIGHT", then it will assume that the top-right corner is rounded but all other corners are square. Also goes for "CORNER-TOPLEFT", "CORNER-BOTTOMLEFT", and "CORNER-BOTTOMRIGHT".
------------------------------------------------------------------------
r875 | ckknight | 2007-01-24 09:45:57 +0000 (Wed, 24 Jan 2007) | 4 lines
Changed paths:
   M /tmp/trunk/Cartographer/Modules/Notes.lua

Cartographer-Notes:
- added square minimap support
Note: minimap shape is determined by a global function: GetMinimapShape() which should return "ROUND" or "SQUARE", if it doesn't exist, "ROUND" is assumed. Minimap addons such as simpleMinimap should be updated to follow this spec.

Cartographer-Notes:
 - colors are no longer stored as r, g, b all as numbers [0, 1], it saves it as a color [0, 16777215] such that ("%06x"):format(color) returns rrggbb in hex. White is considered default and not stored in the DB.
- DB version bumped to 3.
- Note: the API didn't change and if one were to feed in titleR, titleG, titleB as before, it would be converted automatically to the new form.
